					<a href="https://www.simplygreenhome.com/indoor-plants-with-drainage/">

Drainage is critical to prevent root rot. What to Look For Potting Tips Choosing the right “pots with drainage holes” is an easy way to protect your plant and help it thrive indoors.                                         															<h2 class="entry-title">
					<a href="https://www.simplygreenhome.com/care-for-dormant-houseplants/">
						How to Care for Dormant Houseplants in Winter					</a>

                                                                            <div class="elementskit-post-footer">

Dormancy is normal but confusing for beginners. Plants That Go Dormant During dormancy, reduce watering and avoid fertilizing.
